**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-cross-k8s-arch-001: Kubernetes CRD Lifecycle (Cross-Repo)

## Task

Trace how a Custom Resource Definition (CRD) flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem: from CRD type definitions and validation, through etcd storage and the dynamic HTTP handler, to the generated client, informers, listers, and the dynamic client. Map the complete lifecycle across four logical sub-projects within the Kubernetes monorepo.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.30.0 (mirror of kubernetes/kubernetes) (Go, ~2.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding (cross-repo)
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/, staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/, staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/, staging/src/k8s.io/api/

## Architecture Overview

Kubernetes uses a staging directory structure where four logically separate projects coexist in one monorepo:

1. **apiextensions-apiserver** — CRD type definitions, validation, etcd storage, dynamic HTTP handler
2. **client-go** — Generated typed clients, informers, listers, and the dynamic client
3. **apimachinery** — Runtime scheme, GVK/GVR types, ObjectMeta, Unstructured representation
4. **api** — Internal hub types and group registration

## Requirements

1. Trace the CRD type definition layer: internal hub types, external v1 types, and Scheme registration
2. Map the server-side lifecycle: validation, etcd storage, and the dynamic customresource_handler
3. Trace the client-side access layer: typed clientset, SharedIndexInformer, Lister, and DynamicClient
4. Identify the foundational types in apimachinery that everything depends on: Scheme, GVK/GVR, TypeMeta/ObjectMeta, Unstructured

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Foundation: apimachinery types (Scheme, GVK, ObjectMeta, Unstructured)
2. Type definitions: apiextensions types (internal hub + external v1 + registration)
3. Server-side: validation -> etcd storage -> HTTP handler
4. Client-side: typed client -> informer -> lister -> dynamic client
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Cross-project dependency flow
- How CRD types bridge the four sub-projects
- The role of Scheme and GVK in type registration
- How Unstructured enables dynamic custom resource access
- The checkpoint between server-side storage and client-side informer caching]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary of the CRD lifecycle across the K8s ecosystem]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find files across ALL four sub-projects?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct cross-project dependency chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you identify how the sub-projects integrate?

The analysis has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`. Here is a summary of what was traced:

---

## CRD Lifecycle Summary

### Four Sub-Projects and Their Roles

| Sub-project | Role |
|---|---|
| **apimachinery** | Universal vocabulary: `runtime.Scheme`, `schema.GVK/GVR`, `metav1.TypeMeta/ObjectMeta`, `unstructured.Unstructured` |
| **apiextensions-apiserver** | CRD type definitions (hub + v1 + v1beta1), validation, etcd storage (CRD meta + CR instances), dynamic HTTP handler |
| **client-go** | `DynamicClient` (GVR-addressed, Unstructured-based), `dynamicSharedInformerFactory`, `cache.SharedIndexInformer` infrastructure |
| **api** | Standard API group patterns (e.g., `autoscaling/v1.Scale` used by CRD scale subresource); demonstrates hub→versioned→registration lifecycle that CRDs follow |

### Key Dependency Chain

1. **Foundation**: `apimachinery` — `runtime.Scheme` maps Go types ↔ GVKs; `Unstructured` = `map[string]interface{}` carrying any JSON without a compiled struct
2. **Type defs**: `apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/` — internal hub type + v1/v1beta1 external types all registered via `install.Install(scheme)`
3. **Server-side**:
   - Validation: `apiserver/validation` — OpenAPI/CEL structural schema check
   - CRD storage: `registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` — persists the CRD meta-object itself
   - CR storage: `registry/customresource/etcd.go` — stores CR instances as `Unstructured`
   - HTTP routing: `apiserver/customresource_handler.go` — `crdHandler` dynamically provisions per-CRD REST storage, reads CRDs via `CustomResourceDefinitionLister`
4. **Client-side**:
   - Generated typed clientset → `SharedIndexInformer` → `CustomResourceDefinitionLister` (for the CRD meta-object)
   - `DynamicClient` → `dynamicSharedInformerFactor
... (truncated)

`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` \u2014 Initialises the apiextensions apiserver; calls `install.Install(Scheme)`, registers unversioned types; wires CRD REST `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` \u2014 `CustomResourceStorage` with REST, StatusREST, ScaleREST; stores CRs as `unstructured.Unstructured`; scale subresource reads/writes replicas into unstructured fields\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/strategy.go` \u2014 Strategy for custom resource instances; structural schema enforcement, pruning, defaulting, CEL validation\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` \u2014 `crdHandler` HTTP handler; dynamically routes `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>` to per-CRD `customResource` REST storage; holds `crdLister` to discover active CRDs; uses `Unstructured` throughout\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver (Client-Side \u2014 generated)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go` \u2014 Generated `Clientset` implementing typed interface for `ApiextensionsV1` and `ApiextensionsV1beta1`; backed by `client-go/rest`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/informers/externalversions/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` \u2014 Generated `CustomResourceDefinitionInformer`; creates `cache.SharedIndexInformer` with List/Watch from typed clientset; exposes `Lister()`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` \u2014 Generated `CustomResourceDefinitionLister`; reads from `cache.Indexer` (in-memory, populated by informer); returns typed `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition`\n\n### client-go (Dynamic Client + Generic Informer Infrastructure)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/interface.go` \u2014 `Interface` (Resource \u2192 NamespaceableResourceInterface) and `ResourceInterface` (CRUD, Watch, Patch, Apply); all methods operate on `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` \u2014 `DynamicClient` implementation backed by `rest.Interface`; takes `schema.GroupVersionResource` to build HTTP paths; all responses decoded as Unstructured\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` \u2014 `dynamicSharedInformerFactory`; `ForResource(gvr)` creates generic informers keyed by GVR; uses `dynamic.Interface` + `dynamiclister` for GVR-addressed cache\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` \u2014 `ResourceLister` / `NamespaceLister` over `cache.Indexer`; returns `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n\n### api (Built-in Type Patterns + Scale Dependency)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/autoscaling/v1/` \u2014 `Scale` type used by `customresource/etcd.go` ScaleREST; demonstrates the pattern where CRD scale subresources project into a standard autoscaling type\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/`, `apps/v1/`, etc. \u2014 Define the canonical pattern: internal hub type \u2192 external versioned type \u2192 Scheme registration \u2192 REST storage; CRDs follow the exact same pattern, but dynamically\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Foundation \u2014 apimachinery**\n   - `schema.GroupVersionKind` / `GroupVersionResource` \u2014 the universal address space for all Kubernetes types\n   - `runtime.Scheme` \u2014 bidirectional registry mapping Go types \u2194 GVKs; central to encoding/decoding\n   - `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta` \u2014 embedded in every persisted API object\n   - `unstructured.Unstructured` \u2014 `map[string]interface{}` representation that can hold any API object without a registered Go struct\n\n2. **Type Definitions \u2014 apiextensions-apiserver**\n   - Internal hub type (`apiextensions.CustomResourceDefinition`) registered with `SchemeGroupVersion = apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n   - External v1 type (`v1.CustomResourceDefinition`) registered with `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`; embeds `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta`\n   - `install.Install(scheme)` registers all versions and sets priority: v1 > v1beta1\n\n3. **Server-Side \u2014 validation \u2192 etcd storage \u2192 HTTP handler**\n   - **Validation**: `apiserver/validation.SchemaValidator` validates CR instances against the CRD's OpenAPI schema before admission\n   - **CRD etcd storage** (`registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go`): Generic store backed by etcd via `genericregistry.Store`; persists `CustomResourceDefinition` meta-objects; adds cleanup finalizer on delete\n   - **CR etcd storage** (`registry/customresource/etcd.go`): Separate generic store for actual custom resource instances; `NewFunc` returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` pre-tagged with GVK; `ScaleREST` projects replica paths into `autoscaling/v1.Scale`\n   - **HTTP handler** (`apiserver/customresource_handler.go`): `crdHandler` HTTP filter dynamically builds and caches per-CRD `customResourceStorage` when a CRD becomes established; routes `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>` requests; reads CRD state via `listers.CustomResourceDefinitionLister`\n\n4. **Client-Side \u2014 typed client \u2192 informer \u2192 lister \u2192 dynamic client**\n   - **Typed clientset** (`client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go`): Generated code; `ApiextensionsV1()` gives access to `CustomResourceDefinitions()` CRUD methods; uses `client-go/rest` under the hood\n   - **SharedIndexInformer** (`client/informers/.../customresourcedefinition.go`): Uses the typed clientset's List/Watch to populate an in-memory `cache.Indexer`; shared across all consumers to minimise API server load\n   - **Lister** (`client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go`): Read-only view over the informer's `cache.Indexer`; `Get(name)` returns `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition` without an API server round-trip\n   - **DynamicClient** (`client-go/dynamic/simple.go`): GVR-addressed client that sends/receives raw JSON; all objects as `*unstructured.Unstructured`; used by controllers that manage arbitrary CRs without compiled-in type knowledge\n   - **Dynamic informer** (`client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/`): Like typed informers but keyed by `schema.GroupVersionResource`; enables watching arbitrary CRs generically\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 runtime.Scheme         \u2190\u2500\u2500 used by ALL other sub-projects\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 schema.GVK / GVR       \u2190\u2500\u2500 universal type address\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 metav1.TypeMeta/ObjectMeta \u2190\u2500\u2500 embedded in every API object\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 unstructured.Unstructured  \u2190\u2500\u2500 dynamic CR representation\n         \u2193\napiextensions-apiserver\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 types.go (hub + v1)    \u2190\u2500\u2500 CRD Go structs, embed apimachinery types\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 register.go / install  \u2190\u2500\u2500 Scheme registration\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 validation             \u2190\u2500\u2500 structural schema, CEL, OpenAPI validation\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 registry/crd/etcd.go   \u2190\u2500\u2500 CRD meta-object persistence in etcd\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 registry/cr/etcd.go    \u2190\u2500\u2500 CR instance persistence via Unstructured\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 apiserver/handler.go   \u2190\u2500\u2500 dynamic HTTP routing, uses listers\n         \u2193\nclient-go\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 dynamic.Interface      \u2190\u2500\u2500 GVR-addressed, Unstructured-based client\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 dynamic/informer       \u2190\u2500\u2500 generic informer for any GVR\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 tools/cache            \u2190\u2500\u2500 SharedIndexInformer, Indexer (shared infra)\n         \u2191\napiextensions-apiserver (generated clients)\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 clientset              \u2190\u2500\u2500 typed client wrapping client-go/rest\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 informers (generated)  \u2190\u2500\u2500 typed SharedIndexInformer\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 listers (generated)    \u2190\u2500\u2500 typed read from Indexer\n```\n\n### How CRD Types Bridge the Four Sub-Projects\n\nThe `CustomResourceDefinition` object itself follows the universal Kubernetes object pattern established by `apimachinery`: it embeds `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta` from `apimachinery`, is registered in `runtime.Scheme` (also from `apimachinery`), and is persisted through `genericregistry.Store`. This means a CRD object is handled identically to a Pod or Deployment at the storage level\u2014the only difference is its *effect*: a CRD object's existence causes the apiextensions-apiserver to dynamically provision a new REST endpoint for the custom resource kind it describes.\n\nThe custom resource *instances* (CR data) live entirely as `unstructured.Unstructured` throughout their server-side lifecycle. There are no compiled-in Go structs for user-defined CRs. The `crdHandler` HTTP layer reads the CRD spec (via lister \u2192 informer \u2192 typed clientset), constructs a schema validator and storage, and routes all CRUD operations through `customresource/etcd.go`, which stores and retrieves raw JSON documents as `Unstructured` maps.\n\n### The Role of Scheme and GVK in Type Registration\n\n`runtime.Scheme` is the central registry. When `install.Install(scheme)` is called at apiserver startup, it registers three versions of `CustomResourceDefinition`:\n- The internal hub type under `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n- The v1 external type under `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`\n- The v1beta1 external type under `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1beta1`\n\nThe Scheme's `gvkToType` and `typeToGVK` maps enable the codec factory to decode incoming API requests (regardless of version) into the hub type for validation and storage, and to encode outgoing responses into the client's preferred version. Version priority (`v1 > v1beta1`) is also stored in the Scheme and governs which version the API server advertises as preferred.\n\nFor *custom resource instances*, no Scheme registration occurs (there are no Go structs). Instead, the `crdHandler` constructs a runtime codec that directly serializes/deserializes JSON into `Unstructured` maps, bypassing the Scheme for the data plane.\n\n### How Unstructured Enables Dynamic Custom Resource Access\n\n`unstructured.Unstructured` implements both `runtime.Object` (so it can flow through the generic apiserver machinery) and `metav1.Object` (so standard metadata accessors like `GetName()`, `GetUID()`, `GetLabels()` work correctly). Its backing store is a plain `map[string]interface{}`, which can represent any JSON document without needing a compiled Go type.\n\nThe `DynamicClient` in `client-go/dynamic` exploits this: it takes a `schema.GroupVersionResource` at runtime, constructs the URL path, and returns `*unstructured.Unstructured` for all operations. This makes it the primary API for controllers that manage arbitrary CRs (e.g., operator frameworks, GitOps controllers). The `dynamicSharedInformerFactory` builds on top of this, providing a watch-based cache keyed by GVR.\n\n### The Checkpoint Between Server-Side Storage and Client-Side Informer Caching\n\nThe critical checkpoint is the **List/Watch API**. When a `CustomResourceDefinitionInformer` starts, it calls:\n1. `client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().List(...)` \u2014 initial sync, populates the local `cache.Indexer`\n2. `client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().Watch(...)` \u2014 ongoing watch stream, incrementally updates the Indexer\n\nThe `crdHandler` server-side also uses a `CustomResourceDefinitionLister` (backed by its own informer) to read established CRDs without round-tripping to etcd on every request. This means there are two informer caches: one inside the apiextensions-apiserver process (server-side, for routing), and one in any external controller process (client-side, for reconciliation). Both subscribe to the same etcd-backed watch stream.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nA Custom Resource Definition flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem in two distinct planes: the **CRD meta-object plane** (the CRD itself, persisted as a typed Go struct through `genericregistry.Store` backed by etcd) and the **CR instance plane** (actual custom resource data, handled entirely as `unstructured.Unstructured` with no compiled-in Go types). `apimachinery` provides the universal vocabulary\u2014`Scheme`, `GVK/GVR`, `TypeMeta/ObjectMeta`, and `Unstructured`\u2014that all four sub-projects share; `apiextensions-apiserver` implements the CRD type definitions, validation, storage, and dynamic HTTP routing; and `client-go` provides both the generated typed clients/informers/listers for the CRD meta-objects and the generic `DynamicClient` + `dynamicSharedInformerFactory` that let controllers manage arbitrary custom resource instances by GVR at runtime.\n",

The CRD object is thus handled identically to a Pod or Deployment at the storage level\u2014the only difference is its *effect*: a CRD object's existence causes the apiextensions-apiserver's `crdHandler` to dynamically provision a new REST endpoint group for the custom resource kind it describes.\n\nCustom resource *instances* (CR data) live entirely as `unstructured.Unstructured` throughout their server-side lifecycle. implements `runtime.Object`, `metav1.Object`, and `metav1.ListInterface`; the universal carrier for custom resource instances\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver (CRD Type Definitions + Server-Side Lifecycle)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go` \u2014 Internal hub type `CustomResourceDefinition` (embeds `metav1.TypeMeta`) and `CustomResourceDefinitionSpec` with group, names, scope, validation, conversion, versions fields\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/register.go` \u2014 Registers hub types with `runtime.Scheme` under `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`; defines `SchemeGroupVersion`, `SchemeBuilder`, `AddToScheme`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go` \u2014 External v1 `CustomResourceDefinition` (embeds both `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta`); the type users apply to the cluster\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1beta1/types.go` \u2014 Deprecated v1beta1 external type; preserved for backwards compatibility\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/install/install.go` \u2014 Calls `AddToScheme` for internal, v1, v1beta1 types; sets v1 > v1beta1 version priority in Scheme\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` \u2014 Initialises the apiextensions apiserver; calls `install.Install(Scheme)`, registers unversioned types; wires CRD REST storage, controllers, and informer factory\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/validation/validation.go` \u2014 `SchemaValidator` / `SchemaCreateValidator` interfaces; OpenAPI-based structural schema validation via `kube-openapi/pkg/validation`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go` \u2014 `REST` struct wrapping `genericregistry.Store`; etcd-backed storage for `CustomResourceDefinition` meta-objects; adds cleanup finalizer on delete\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresourcedefinition/strategy.go` \u2014 Strategy (PrepareForCreate, PrepareForUpdate, Validate, Canonicalize) for CRD meta-objects\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/etcd.go` \u2014 `CustomResourceStorage` with REST, StatusREST, ScaleREST; stores CRs as `unstructured.Unstructured`; scale subresource reads/writes replica counts via nested unstructured field access\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/registry/customresource/strategy.go` \u2014 Strategy for custom resource instances; structural schema enforcement, pruning, defaulting, CEL validation\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` \u2014 `crdHandler` HTTP handler; dynamically routes `/apis/<group>/<version>/<resource>` to per-CRD REST storage; holds `listers.CustomResourceDefinitionLister` to discover active CRDs; uses `Unstructured` throughout\n\n### apiextensions-apiserver (Generated Client-Side)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go` \u2014 Generated `Clientset`; `ApiextensionsV1()` exposes typed CRUD for `CustomResourceDefinitions`; backed by `client-go/rest`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/informers/externalversions/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` \u2014 Generated `CustomResourceDefinitionInformer`; creates `cache.SharedIndexInformer` with List/Watch from typed clientset; exposes `Lister()`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go` \u2014 Generated `CustomResourceDefinitionLister`; reads from `cache.Indexer` (in-memory, populated by informer); returns typed `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition` with no API server round-trip\n\n### client-go (Dynamic Client + Generic Informer Infrastructure)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/interface.go` \u2014 `Interface` (Resource(gvr) \u2192 NamespaceableResourceInterface) and `ResourceInterface` (Create, Update, Get, List, Watch, Patch, Apply, Delete); all methods operate on `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/simple.go` \u2014 `DynamicClient` implementation backed by `rest.Interface`; takes `schema.GroupVersionResource` to build HTTP paths dynamically; all responses decoded as Unstructured\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go` \u2014 `dynamicSharedInformerFactory`; `ForResource(gvr)` creates generic informers keyed by GVR; uses `dynamic.Interface` for List/Watch and `dynamiclister` for cache access\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/dynamic/dynamiclister/lister.go` \u2014 `ResourceLister` / `NamespaceLister` over `cache.Indexer`; returns `*unstructured.Unstructured`\n\n### api (Built-in API Patterns + Scale Dependency)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/autoscaling/v1/` \u2014 `Scale` type used by `customresource/etcd.go` `ScaleREST`; CRD scale subresources project unstructured replica fields into this standard type\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/`, `apps/v1/`, etc. \u2014 Define the canonical pattern that CRDs replicate: internal hub type \u2192 external versioned type \u2192 Scheme registration \u2192 REST storage; the `api` sub-project demonstrates the standard group registration lifecycle that `apiextensions-apiserver` follows for CRD objects themselves\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Foundation \u2014 apimachinery types (Scheme, GVK, ObjectMeta, Unstructured)**\n   - `schema.GroupVersionKind` / `GroupVersionResource` \u2014 universal address space for all Kubernetes types\n   - `runtime.Scheme` \u2014 bidirectional registry mapping Go types \u2194 GVKs; central to encoding/decoding across all sub-projects\n   - `metav1.TypeMeta` + `metav1.ObjectMeta` \u2014 embedded in every persisted API object, including `CustomResourceDefinition` itself\n   - `unstructured.Unstructured` \u2014 `map[string]interface{}` representation enabling the server to handle arbitrary custom resource data without compiled-in Go structs\n\n2. **Type Definitions \u2014 apiextensions types (internal hub + external v1 + registration)**\n   - Internal hub `CustomResourceDefinition` registered at `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n   - External v1 `CustomResourceDefinition` registered at `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1` (embeds TypeMeta + ObjectMeta from apimachinery)\n   - `install.Install(scheme)` registers all versions and sets priority: v1 > v1beta1\n   - Group constant `GroupName = \"apiextensions.k8s.io\"` and `SchemeGroupVersion` wired via `schema.GroupVersion` from apimachinery\n\n3. **Server-Side \u2014 validation \u2192 etcd storage \u2192 HTTP handler**\n   - **Validation** (`apiserver/validation`): `SchemaValidator.Validate()` checks CR instances against the CRD's OpenAPI v3 structural schema before write; `ValidateUpdate()` supports ratcheting for backwards-compatible changes\n   - **CRD etcd storage** (`registry/customresourcedefinition/etcd.go`): `genericregistry.Store` backed by etcd; persists `CustomResourceDefinition` meta-objects; REST strategy runs validation + defaulting; adds `customresourcecleanup.apiextensions.k8s.io` finalizer on delete to ensure CR cleanup\n   - **CR etcd storage** (`registry/customresource/etcd.go`): Separate `genericregistry.Store` for actual custom resource instances; `NewFunc` returns `&unstructured.Unstructured{}` pre-tagged with the CRD's GVK; `ScaleREST` projects replica paths into `autoscaling/v1.Scale` for HPA integration\n   - **HTTP handler** (`apiserver/customresource_handler.go`): `crdHandler` is a filter that dynamically provisions per-CRD REST storage when a CRD becomes established (via `listers.CustomResourceDefinitionLister`); routes incoming HTTP requests to the appropriate storage; uses apimachinery serializers over Unstructured for encode/decode\n\n4. **Client-Side \u2014 typed client \u2192 informer \u2192 lister \u2192 dynamic client**\n   - **Typed clientset** (`client/clientset/clientset/clientset.go`): Generated code wrapping `client-go/rest`; provides `ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions()` with List, Get, Create, Update, Watch\n   - **SharedIndexInformer** (`client/informers/.../customresourcedefinition.go`): Calls typed clientset List/Watch to keep an in-memory `cache.Indexer` populated; shared across consumers to reduce API server load\n   - **Lister** (`client/listers/apiextensions/v1/customresourcedefinition.go`): Read-only view over `cache.Indexer`; `Get(name)` returns `*v1.CustomResourceDefinition` from local cache\n   - **DynamicClient** (`client-go/dynamic/simple.go`): GVR-addressed; uses apimachinery's `schema.GroupVersionResource` to build URL paths at runtime; returns `*unstructured.Unstructured`; primary API for operator frameworks managing arbitrary CRs\n   - **Dynamic informer** (`client-go/dynamic/dynamicinformer/`): `ForResource(gvr)` creates a `cache.SharedIndexInformer` using `DynamicClient` List/Watch; enables watch-based caching of any CR type without a compiled-in Go struct\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Cross-Project Dependency Flow\n\n```\napimachinery\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 runtime.Scheme            \u2190 used by ALL sub-projects for type registration\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 schema.GVK / GVR          \u2190 universal type address, used everywhere\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 metav1.TypeMeta/ObjectMeta\u2190 embedded in every API object\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 unstructured.Unstructured \u2190 dynamic CR representation, core of CR data plane\n         |\n         v\napiextensions-apiserver\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 types.go (hub + v1)       \u2190 CRD Go structs, embed apimachinery types\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 register.go / install     \u2190 Scheme registration (AddToScheme, SetVersionPriority)\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 apiserver/validation      \u2190 structural schema, CEL, OpenAPI validation\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 registry/crd/etcd.go      \u2190 CRD meta-object persistence in etcd\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 registry/cr/etcd.go       \u2190 CR instance persistence via Unstructured\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 apiserver/handler.go      \u2190 dynamic HTTP routing; reads CRDs via listers\n         |\n         v (uses client-go/rest and cache infrastructure)\nclient-go\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 dynamic.Interface         \u2190 GVR-addressed, Unstructured-based CRUD\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 dynamic/informer          \u2190 generic informer for any GVR\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 tools/cache               \u2190 SharedIndexInformer, Indexer (shared infrastructure)\n         ^\n         | (generated clients import client-go)\napiextensions-apiserver (generated client-side)\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 clientset                 \u2190 typed client wrapping client-go/rest\n  \u251c\u2500\u2500 informers (generated)     \u2190 typed SharedIndexInformer for CRD objects\n  \u2514\u2500\u2500 listers (generated)       \u2190 typed read from Indexer\n```\n\n### How CRD Types Bridge the Four Sub-Projects\n\nThe `CustomResourceDefinition` object follows the universal pattern established by `apimachinery`: it embeds `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta`, is registered in `runtime.Scheme`, and is persisted through `genericregistry.Store`. The CRD object is thus handled identically to a Pod or Deployment at the storage level\u2014the only difference is its *effect*: a CRD object's existence causes the apiextensions-apiserver's `crdHandler` to dynamically provision a new REST endpoint group for the custom resource kind it describes.\n\nCustom resource *instances* (CR data) live entirely as `unstructured.Unstructured` throughout their server-side lifecycle. There are no compiled-in Go structs for user-defined types. The `crdHandler` reads the CRD spec via a `CustomResourceDefinitionLister` (itself backed by a generated informer and typed clientset), constructs a schema validator and `customResourceStorage`, and routes all CRUD operations through `customresource/etcd.go`, which stores and retrieves raw JSON as `Unstructured` maps.\n\n### The Role of Scheme and GVK in Type Registration\n\n`runtime.Scheme` is the central registry. When `install.Install(scheme)` is called at apiserver startup:\n- The internal hub type is registered under `apiextensions.k8s.io/__internal`\n- The v1 external type under `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1`\n- The v1beta1 external type under `apiextensions.k8s.io/v1beta1`\n- Version priority is set: v1 > v1beta1\n\nThe Scheme's `gvkToType` and `typeToGVK` maps enable the codec factory to decode incoming API requests (regardless of version) into the hub type for validation and storage, and to encode outgoing responses into the client's requested version.\n\nFor *custom resource instances*, no Scheme registration occurs. Instead, `crdHandler` builds a runtime codec that directly serializes/deserializes JSON into `Unstructured` maps, bypassing the Scheme for the CR data plane. The GVK is carried inside the Unstructured's `Object[\"apiVersion\"]` and `Object[\"kind\"]` fields.\n\n### How Unstructured Enables Dynamic Custom Resource Access\n\n`unstructured.Unstructured` implements both `runtime.Object` (allowing it to flow through the generic apiserver machinery unchanged) and `metav1.Object` (so standard metadata accessors like `GetName()`, `GetUID()`, `GetLabels()` work correctly via nested map traversal). Its backing store is a `map[string]interface{}` that can represent any JSON document.\n\nThe `DynamicClient` exploits this: it takes a `schema.GroupVersionResource` at runtime, constructs the URL path, serializes/deserializes JSON, and returns `*unstructured.Unstructured`. This makes it the primary API for controllers that manage arbitrary CRs without advance knowledge of the schema. The `dynamicSharedInformerFactory` builds on top, providing a watch-based cache keyed by GVR so controllers can avoid repeated API server calls.\n\n### The Checkpoint Between Server-Side Storage and Client-Side Informer Caching\n\nThe critical bridge is the **List/Watch API endpoint**. When a `CustomResourceDefinitionInformer` starts, it executes:\n1. `client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().List(...)` \u2014 performs an initial bulk sync, populating the local `cache.Indexer` with all current CRDs\n2. `client.ApiextensionsV1().CustomResourceDefinitions().Watch(...)` \u2014 subscribes to an etcd watch stream; incremental Add/Update/Delete events keep the Indexer current\n\nThe `crdHandler` server-side also holds its own `CustomResourceDefinitionLister` (backed by an internal informer) to look up established CRDs on every request without hitting etcd directly. This means there are two independent informer caches: one inside the apiextensions-apiserver process (for HTTP routing decisions) and one in any external controller process (for reconciliation logic). Both subscribe to the same underlying etcd watch stream through the API server's watch-cache layer.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nA Custom Resource Definition flows through the Kubernetes ecosystem across two planes: the **CRD meta-object plane**, where the CRD itself is a typed Go struct persisted through `genericregistry.Store` into etcd and accessed via generated clientsets, informers, and listers; and the **CR instance plane**, where actual custom resource data is handled entirely as `unstructured.Unstructured` with no compiled-in Go types, routed dynamically by `crdHandler` using GVK/GVR from apimachinery's schema package. `apimachinery` provides the universal vocabulary\u2014`Scheme`, `GVK/GVR`, `TypeMeta/ObjectMeta`, and `Unstructured`\u2014that all four sub-projects depend on; `apiextensions-apiserver` implements the CRD type definitions, validation pipeline, dual etcd storage layers (one for CRD meta-objects, one for CR instances), and dynamic HTTP routing; and `client-go` supplies both the generated typed clients/informers/listers for managing CRD objects and the generic `DynamicClient`/`dynamicSharedInformerFactory` that let controllers watch and reconcile arbitrary custom resource instances by GVR at runtime.\n",
